### `ActiveRequestLimitsConfig`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/ActiveRequestLimitsConfig.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class ActiveRequestLimitsConfig(active: Map[String, NonNegativeInt] = Map.empty, warnOnUndefinedLimits: Boolean = false, throttleLoggingRatePerSecond: NonNegativeInt = NonNegativeInt.tryCreate(10)) extends UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Configuration to limit the number of open requests per service

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-adminserverconfig"></a>

### `AdminServerConfig`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/AdminServerConfig.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class AdminServerConfig(address: String = defaultAddress, internalPort: Option[Port] = None, tls: Option[TlsServerConfig] = None, jwtTimestampLeeway: Option[JwtTimestampLeeway] = None, keepAliveServer: Option[BasicKeepAliveServerConfig] = Some( BasicKeepAliveServerConfig() ), maxInboundMessageSize: NonNegativeInt = ServerConfig.defaultMaxInboundMessageSize, authServices: Seq[AuthServiceConfig] = Seq.empty, adminTokenConfig: AdminTokenConfig = AdminTokenConfig(), maxTokenLifetime: NonNegativeDuration = NonNegativeDuration(5.minutes), jwksCacheConfig: JwksCacheConfig = JwksCacheConfig(), limits: Option[ActiveRequestLimitsConfig] = None) extends ServerConfig with UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

A variant of ServerConfig that by default listens to connections only on the loopback interface.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-cantonconfigprevalidator"></a>

### `CantonConfigPrevalidator`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/CantonConfigPrevalidator.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait CantonConfigPrevalidator[-A] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

Type class for the validation checks that are specific for a particular configuration class. Unlike CantonConfigValidator, the checks performed by instances of this type class do not recurse into subconfigurations.

**Members**

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-cantonconfigutil"></a>

### `CantonConfigUtil`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/CantonConfigUtil$.html)

**Signature**

```text
object CantonConfigUtil
```

**Summary**

By default pureconfig will expect our H2 config to use the value h-2 for type. This just changes this expectation to being lower cased so h2 will work.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-cantonconfigvalidator"></a>

### `CantonConfigValidator`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/CantonConfigValidator.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait CantonConfigValidator[A] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

Type class for validations of Canton config classes depending on CantonEditions. Instances are typically derived using manual.CantonConfigValidatorDerivation via Magnolia so that validation automatically calls validate on the subconfigurations, where the subconfigurations of A are all the types of fields of a case class that implements A. The derivation must find a corresponding CantonConfigPrevalidator instance via implicit resolution.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-retentionperioddefaults"></a>

### `RetentionPeriodDefaults`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/RetentionPeriodDefaults.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class RetentionPeriodDefaults(sequencer: NonNegativeFiniteDuration = config.NonNegativeFiniteDuration.ofDays(7), mediator: NonNegativeFiniteDuration = config.NonNegativeFiniteDuration.ofDays(7)) extends UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Default retention periods used by pruning commands where no values are explicitly specified. Although by default the commands will retain enough data to remain operational, however operators may like to retain more than this to facilitate possible disaster recovery scenarios or retain evidence of completed transactions.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-sessionencryptionkeycacheconfig"></a>

### `SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig(enabled: Boolean = true, senderCache: CacheConfigWithTimeout = CacheConfigWithTimeout( maximumSize = PositiveNumeric.tryCreate(10000), expireAfterTimeout = PositiveFiniteDuration.ofSeconds(10), ), receiverCache: CacheConfigWithTimeout = CacheConfigWithTimeout( maximumSize = PositiveNumeric.tryCreate(10000), expireAfterTimeout = PositiveFiniteDuration.ofSeconds(10), )) extends UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Configuration settings for a cache that stores: (a) the public asymmetric encryptions of the session keys for the sender and (b) the decrypting results in the receiver. This reduces the amount of asymmetric operations that need to be performed for each of the views that share the same participant recipient group (i.e. use the same session key).

**Members**

| Docs | Member | Introduced | Deprecated | Removed |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig.html#enabled:Boolean) | `enabled: Boolean` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig.html#receiverCache:com.digitalasset.canton.config.CacheConfigWithTimeout) | `receiverCache: CacheConfigWithTimeout` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig.html#senderCache:com.digitalasset.canton.config.CacheConfigWithTimeout) | `senderCache: CacheConfigWithTimeout` | `3.4.10` | - | - |
| [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig$.html#sessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfigCantonConfigValidator:com.digitalasset.canton.config.CantonConfigValidator[com.digitalasset.canton.config.SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig]) | `sessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfigCantonConfigValidator: CantonConfigValidator[SessionEncryptionKeyCacheConfig]` | `3.4.10` | - | - |

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-sessionsigningkeysconfig"></a>

### `SessionSigningKeysConfig`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/SessionSigningKeysConfig.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class SessionSigningKeysConfig(enabled: Boolean, keyValidityDuration: PositiveFiniteDuration = PositiveFiniteDuration.ofMinutes(5), cutOffDuration: PositiveFiniteDuration = PositiveFiniteDuration.ofSeconds(30), keyEvictionPeriod: PositiveFiniteDuration = PositiveFiniteDuration.ofMinutes(10), signingAlgorithmSpec: SigningAlgorithmSpec = SigningAlgorithmSpec.Ed25519, signingKeySpec: SigningKeySpec = SigningKeySpec.EcCurve25519) extends PrettyPrinting with UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Configuration for enabling session signing keys with a specified validity period. This setting is applicable only when using a KMS provider with externally stored keys.

**Members**

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-config-watchdogconfig"></a>

### `WatchdogConfig`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/WatchdogConfig.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class WatchdogConfig(enabled: Boolean, checkInterval: PositiveFiniteDuration = PositiveFiniteDuration(15.seconds), killDelay: NonNegativeFiniteDuration = NonNegativeFiniteDuration(30.seconds)) extends UniformCantonConfigValidation with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Returns all validation errors that are specific to this Canton configuration class. Successful validation should return an empty sequence.
